9-32 Decklists
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on November 1, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/hero/wizardslogo_thumb.jpg)
By Corbin Hosler and Marc Calderaro











The Standard is much than just the Top 8. We'd be remiss if we didn't give you some of the great decks that fell just shy of the final phase—some by mere percentage points.


Below are the 9th through 32nd place decks. Enjoy!







#### Kent Ketter's Dark Jeskai – 9th, Grand Prix Indianapolis


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-46548868cd7d75f7e7259e88dabf96ee?n=Kent%20Ketter%27s%20Dark%20Jeskai%20%E2%80%93%209th%2C%20Grand%20Prix%20Indianapolis)

#### Andrew Cuneo's Esper Control – 31st, Grand Prix Indianapolis
